# <a name="responsecode"></a><span data-ttu-id="52b22-103">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52b22-103">ResponseCode</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52b22-104">Элемент **ResponseCode** предоставляет сведения о состоянии о запросе.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52b22-104">The **ResponseCode** element provides status information about the request.</span></span> 
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="52b22-105">ResponseMessage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52b22-105">ResponseMessage</span></span>](responsemessage.md) 
- [<span data-ttu-id="52b22-106">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52b22-106">ResponseCode</span></span>](responsecode.md)
  
```XML
<ResponseCode/>
```

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="52b22-1480">Замечания</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52b22-1480">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52b22-1481">Этот элемент не является обязательным и не добавляется во все ответы.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52b22-1481">This element is not required and is not included in all responses.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="52b22-1482">Схема, описывающая этот элемент, находится в виртуальном каталоге IIS, в котором размещены веб-службы Exchange.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52b22-1482">The schema that describes this element is located in the IIS virtual directory that hosts Exchange Web Services.</span></span>
